        <script>
            const DateTime = window.luxon.DateTime;

            fetch('https://mixreality.tribexr.com/calendar/schedule/list')
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    const event = data.data.upcoming_events[0];
                    let durationArray = event.duration.split(":").map(x => Number(x));

                    let startDate = DateTime.fromISO(`${event.startDate}T${event.startTime}`, {
                        zone: "utc"
                    });
                    let endDate = startDate.plus({ hours:durationArray[0], minutes: durationArray[1] });
                     let now = DateTime.utc();
                    // let now = DateTime.fromISO(`${event.startDate}T${'18:00:00'}`, {
                    //     zone: "utc"
                    // });
                    let minutesBetweenEndAndNow = endDate.diff(now, 'minutes').toObject().minutes;
                    let minutesBetweenStartAndNow = startDate.diff(now, 'minutes').toObject().minutes;
                    if (minutesBetweenStartAndNow <= 0 && minutesBetweenEndAndNow > 0){
                        document.getElementById('buttonContainer').style.display = "flex";
                        document.getElementById('eventLink').href = event.url;
                    }
                });
        </script>
